ui(detail): overhaul behavioral DNA manifest in EventDetailModal

Standardized and synchronized the display of commitment operational 
metadata to achieve 1:1 parity with the creation flow.

Key Changes:
- Extracted 'Intensity' and 'Allowed Misses' into dedicated, high-fidelity 
  rows within the EventDetail ConfigSection.
- Synchronized iconography with final.tsx: mapped 'speedometer' to 
  Intensity and 'alert-circle-outline' to Allowed Misses.
- Improved logical grouping for 'Stay Throughout' commitments, surfacing 
  the full strictness protocol at a glance.
- Maintained the 42px left-column alignment standard for perfect 
  vertical rhythm across all detail components.

This ensures that users can see the exact enforcement rules (strictness 
and failure thresholds) directly in the event drawer without needing 
to navigate back to the parent task.
